# Latin-script languages (comparison)

Selected character-set databases (CLDR, Latin Plus) juxtaposed next to Rosettaâ€™s Langs DB. When comparing, characters that are included in â€œRosetta (base)â€ are marked grey, any additional characters are marked red. Only â€œbaseâ€ fields are compared. The third column indicates the status of the field (ğŸ”´ = draft/contributed/todo, âš«ï¸ = done, âšªï¸ = unkown).
